			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ALG_strengthen_ENTV_environmental_campaigns"
			# Check if we can build in state 386 (capital) AND have at least one other state with free slots
			if = {
				limit = {
					386 = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
						free_building_slots = {
							building = internet_station
							size > 0
						}
					}
					any_owned_state = {
						NOT = { state = 386 }
						free_building_slots = {
							building = internet_station
							size > 0
						}
					}
				}
				# Full cost - building in two states
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -6 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
				# Build in state 386 (capital)
				386 = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = internet_station
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				# Build in one other random state
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { state = 386 }
						free_building_slots = {
							building = internet_station
							size > 0
						}
					}
					add_building_construction = {
						type = internet_station
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# Can only build in state 386 (capital)
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					386 = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
						free_building_slots = {
							building = internet_station
							size > 0
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -3 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
				386 = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = internet_station
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# Can only build in other states (not capital)
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					any_owned_state = {
						free_building_slots = {
							building = internet_station
							size > 0
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -3 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						free_building_slots = {
							building = internet_station
							size > 0
						}
					}
					add_building_construction = {
						type = internet_station
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# No building slots available anywhere
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 5 }
				change_domestic_influence_percentage = yes
				custom_effect_tooltip = ALG_environmental_campaign_no_space_tt
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
